           angular distributions for En < 1 MeV                   14243  1    4 
AUTHOR     (F.-J.Hambsch,I.Ruskov)                                14243  1    5 
INSTITUTE  (2ZZZGEL,3BULBLA)                                      14243  1    6 
REFERENCE  (J,NSE,163,1,2009)                                     14243  1    7 
FACILITY   (LINAC,2ZZZGEL)Experiment performed at the Geel        14243  1    8 
           Electron Linear Accelerator time-of-flight spectrometer14243  1    9 
SAMPLE     B4C deposit with minimal purity of 98.0% enriched in   14243  1   10 
           B10 to 94.0% with thickness of 14.5(8) and 15.7(8)     14243  1   11 
           mu-g/cm2 and diameter of 84 mm. Two samples of each    14243  1   12 
           thickness were used. B4C deposited on polished         14243  1   13 
           stainless steel foil with thicknes of 0.3mm and        14243  1   14 
           diameter of 100 mm                                     14243  1   15 
DETECTOR   (IOCH)A twin Frisch-grid gas ionization chamber was    14243  1   16 
           used. With this type of detector, a simultaneous       14243  1   17 
           measurement of the energy and angular distribution     14243  1   18 
           of the charged particles from the reaction is          14243  1   19 
           possible in a nearly 2x2Pi geometry.The two boron      14243  1   20 
           samples were mounted in a back-to-back geometry on the 14243  1   21 
           common cathode of the chamber.                         14243  1   22 
METHOD     (TOF) Energy of incident neutrons determined by        14243  1   23 
           time-of-flight                                         14243  1   24 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO)Photoneutrons produced by Bremsstrahlung in     14243  1   25 
           an uranium target. Measurements were performed at      14243  1   26 
           two different flight-path distances from the GELINA    14243  1   27 
           neutron-producing target: L1 = 28.24 m (moderated      14243  1   28 
           beam) and L2 = 57.41 m (unmoderated beam). A B4C       14243  1   29 
           filter was placed in the beam, which effectively       14243  1   30 
           removed neutrons with thermal and epithermal energies. 14243  1   31 
CORRECTION Corrected for different sample thickness (4%) in       14243  1   32 
           backside ion chamber                                   14243  1   33 
HISTORY    (20090818C)Compiled by S.H.                            14243  1   34
